posted:Posted May 19, 2024
msg:Wuxi is a good place, with green mountains and clear waters, and a good climate. During this trip to Wuxi, I stayed at Taihu Hotel, and the experience was very good. I did some research before and learned that this hotel was formerly the site of Jiangnan University. It was officially listed as Taihu Hotel in 1952. It is a well-established five-star hotel with a very long history. It has received more than 60 Chinese and foreign heads of state over the years. The software and hardware are of high standards. As soon as we arrived at the hotel, the handsome doorman wearing a small hat took over the luggage and took us to check in. We booked a garden room with a balcony. Standing on the balcony, we can overlook the tower on the highest mountain of Yuantouzhu. The scenery is very good. If you stay in this hotel, you must go to its back garden, if you have enough time after breakfast. It's so beautiful, a large bamboo forest is lush, the lake is rippling, mandarin ducks are playing in the water, and there are peacocks. Many campers come here in summer, as well as those who take wedding photos and wedding ceremonies. This is indeed a good place. The Chinese restaurant on the 3rd floor tastes very good, but the price is a little high, but this level of service is normal for a hotel. The breakfast buffet is very rich in variety, and every hotel service staff is very friendly. There is also a fireworks show on weekend nights, which is very beautiful. The stay experience is great!!!

The hotel reception staff pay attention to etiquette, hospitality, and proactive service.
Jichangxuan is the hotel's Chinese restaurant. The dishes are very exquisite and high-end, and the environment is elegant. People who like loud noises will be quiet all of a sudden. Wuxi braised spareribs must be tasted. People with an appetite can taste all the three whites of Wuxi here, because it is the most authentic here.
The front desk arranged my room facing Taihu Lake, with pleasant scenery, wide vision, fresh air, birdsong and fragrance of flowers. It is really super enjoyable.
There is a teahouse in the hotel for everyone to enjoy. There is also a high-end custom clothing store. You must stay at Wuxi Taihu Hotel when you come to Wuxi. This is a good choice for you.

No. Hotel.

Knock on the blackboard! Yuantouzhu Fast Track Guide: The biggest value of the hotel ~ Guanshe Villa Cruise Terminal ~ The fast track (speedboat) to Yuantouzhu has a super high gold content. It takes a few minutes to take a taxi from the hotel or walk for less than 20 minutes. Navigate to Guanshe Villa Cruise Terminal That‚Äôs it, if you take a taxi, navigate to Xiaonanguo and get off at the nearest pier. I found out from the site survey of the Raiders before that the so-called Guanshe Villa No. 3 and No. 8 piers are actually the same pier, but No. 8 is dedicated to groups, No. 3 is for individual passengers, and the two ticket gates are next to each other.
It should be noted here that you must buy Yuantouzhu electronic tickets in advance to buy a one-way speedboat ticket of 45 yuan, which is equivalent to entering the park with a ticket when you board the boat. However, the boat ticket seems to be from 8:30--15:30. On the premise that there must be a ticket, line up to buy a paper boat ticket on the spot. If you really plan to enjoy the wild cherry blossoms in the fast track, you must go there early to guard, otherwise there will be no boat. .
